<body>
  <header class="lesson-header">
    <h1>{{lessonTitle}}</h1>
    <div class="lesson-meta">
      <span>Grade: {{gradeLevel}}</span>
      <span>Subject: {{subject}}</span>
      <span>Duration: ~{{estimatedDuration}} min</span>
    </div>
  </header>
  
  <main class="lesson-content">
    {{#stages}}
    <section class="lesson-stage" id="{{id}}">
      <h2>{{title}}</h2>
      <p class="stage-description">{{description}}</p>
      
      <div class="stage-content">
        {{{content}}} <!-- Rich text content from educator -->
      </div>
      
      {{#selectedModule}}
      <div class="stage-module">
        {{{renderedModule}}} <!-- Module rendered per rules above -->
      </div>
      {{/selectedModule}}
    </section>
    {{/stages}}
  </main>
  
  <footer class="lesson-footer">
    <p>Created with NET Lesson Assembler V1.3</p>
    <p>{{createdDate}}</p>
  </footer>
</body>
</html>
`;

const EXPORT_METADATA_SCHEMA = {
  version: "1.0",
  lessonId: "uuid",
  title: "string",
  created: "ISO8601 timestamp",
  author: "string (optional)",
  
  curriculum: {
    gradeLevel: "string",
    subject: "string",
    tags: "array<string>",
    estimatedDuration: "number (minutes)"
  },
  
  structure: {
    templateUsed: "super_lesson_v1",
    stages: [
      {
        id: "string",
        title: "string",
        contentWordCount: "number",
        moduleUsed: {
          id: "number",
          title: "string",
          category: "string",
          configData: "object (the module's filled-in dataSchema)"
        }
      }
    ]
  },
  
  analytics: {
    assemblyTimeMinutes: "number (if tracked)",
    modulesChanged: "number (how many times user swapped modules)",
    revisionCount: "number (saves before final export)"
  }
};

javascriptconst VALIDATION_GATES = {
  
  gate1_AssetCompleteness: {
    dueDate: "Before any V1.3 code is written",
    requirements: [
      {
        check: "All T1_READY modules have complete dataSchema",
        method: "Manual audit of restructured Arsenal",
        passCondition: "100% of T1 modules fully specified"
      },
      {
        check: "Stage-Module compatibility map is complete",
        method: "Every stage has 1 default + 3-4 recommended modules",
        passCondition: "No stage left without valid T1 modules"
      },
      {
        check: "Export rendering rules exist for all T1 componentTypes",
        method: "Can generate static HTML for every module type",
        passCondition: "No module renders as [PLACEHOLDER]"
      }
    ],
    failureAction: "BLOCK development until resolved"
  },
  
  gate2_UserAssumptionValidation: {
    dueDate: "Week 1 of development",
    requirements: [
      {
        check: "5-stage template matches user mental model",
        method: "5 user interviews with target educators",
        questions: [
          "Walk me through how you currently prep a lesson",
          "Do these 5 stages match your process?",
          "What would you rename these stages to be clearer?"
        ],
        passCondition: "4 out of 5 users confirm template is helpful, not constraining"
      },
      {
        check: "Module descriptions are self-explanatory",
        method: "Show 10 T1 modules, ask users to explain what each does",
        passCondition: "8 out of 10 correct explanations without additional help"
      }
    ],
    failureAction: "Revise assets before continuing development"
  },
  
  gate3_TimeSavingsValidation: {
    dueDate: "After V1.3 prototype is functional",
    requirements: [
      {
        check: "V1.3 actually saves time vs. baseline",
        method: "Time 5 users creating same lesson in V1.3 vs. Google Docs",
        metrics: {
          baseline: "Average time in Google Docs (measure first)",
          target: "V1.3 time is 30% less than baseline",
          minimum: "V1.3 time is at least equal to baseline (not slower)"
        },
        passCondition: "Mean V1.3 time < baseline time with p < 0.05"
      }
    ],
    failureAction: {
      ifSlower: "DO NOT LAUNCH. Diagnose bottlenecks, simplify further.",
      ifEqual: "Warning signal. Launch with caution, monitor adoption.",
      ifFaster: "Proceed with confidence."
    }
  }
};

SECTION 6: ANSWERS TO UNASKED CRITICAL QUESTIONS
6.1 "What if the 60-module Arsenal is actually important?"
Question: The audit recommends cutting modules drastically. But what if having a large catalog is a selling point?
Answer:
It's not about having 60 modules—it's about showing 60 modules at once.
Better architecture:

Build all 60 modules (over time, not for MVP)
Show 5-10 modules per stage based on smart filtering
Unlock gradually as users demonstrate competency
Learn from usage data which modules are actually valuable

Analogy: Photoshop has 500+ tools, but the toolbar shows 20. Power users learn keyboard shortcuts for the rest. Your Arsenal needs the same progressive disclosure.
6.2 "What if users hate the 5-stage template?"
Question: What if user validation reveals educators don't think in 5 stages?
Pivot strategy:

Immediate fix: Make template opt-in, provide blank canvas alternative
Data collection: Track which users choose template vs. blank (50/50 split = template is polarizing)
Redesign: If template is rejected, pivot to "lesson blocks" model:

User adds modular sections in any order
Sections are: "Text Content", "Interactive Module", "Assessment", "Discussion Prompt"
No prescribed sequence



When to pivot: If <60% of test users find template helpful in Gate 2 validation.
6.3 "How do we add more modules after V1.3 launches?"
Module addition workflow:
javascriptconst MODULE_ADDITION_PROCESS = {
  step1_Design: {
    create: "Module specification document",
    includes: [
      "dataSchema definition",
      "Compatible stages",
      "Static export rendering rule",
      "Setup time estimate"
    ]
  },
  
  step2_Implement: {
    build: "Module configuration form component",
    test: "Can user fill out form in <5 min?"
  },
  
  step3_ExportRendering: {
    build: "Static HTML template for module",
    test: "Does export look professional?"
  },
  
  step4_Deploy: {
    update: "Arsenal JSON with new module",
    tier: "T1_READY",
    releaseNote: "Announce new module to users"
  },
  
  versioning: {
    backwardCompatibility: "Old lessons still export correctly",
    migration: "Not needed - modules are additive"
  }
};
6.4 "What about collaboration features?"
Question: What if multiple teachers want to work on the same lesson?
V1.3 answer: Not supported. Export/import workflow instead:

Teacher A creates lesson, exports .zip
Teacher A shares .zip file
Teacher B imports .zip into their V1.3
Teacher B edits and re-exports

Why defer: Collaboration requires:

Backend server (no longer browser-only)
Authentication system
Conflict resolution
Real-time sync

This is 3x development scope. Validate single-user value first.
Future (V2.0+): Consider "lesson library" where users can:

Publish lessons to shared repository
Fork others' lessons
Rate and comment


SECTION 7: FINAL STRATEGIC RECOMMENDATIONS
7.1 THE REAL RISK YOU'RE NOT ADDRESSING
The biggest risk isn't technical—it's product-market fit.
Your core assumption: "Educators using AI lesson prep spend MORE time, so a structured tool will save time."
What if: Educators struggling with AI aren't struggling with structure—they're struggling with content quality?
Alternative hypothesis:

AI generates mediocre content quickly
Educator spends time fixing/improving it
The bottleneck is evaluation, not creation

If true: Your V1.3 won't save time because it still requires educators to write/curate all content manually. It's just a fancy template, not a force multiplier.
Recommended validation:
Before investing 6 weeks in V1.3, run this experiment:
javascriptconst VALIDATION_EXPERIMENT = {
  hypothesis: "Structured templates save time vs. blank canvas",
  
  method: "Split test with 10 educators",
  
  groupA: {
    tool: "Google Doc with NET 5-stage template pre-formatted",
    task: "Create a vocabulary lesson"
  },
  
  groupB: {
    tool: "Blank Google Doc",
    task: "Create a vocabulary lesson"
  },
  
  measure: [
    "Time to completion",
    "User satisfaction (1-10)",
    "Quality of output (peer-rated)"
  ],
  
  costToRun: "1 day + $200 for participant incentives",
  
  decision: {
    ifTemplateSlower: "Your product hypothesis is wrong - pivot",
    ifTemplateEqual: "Template isn't the differentiator - what is?",
    ifTemplateFaster: "Proceed with V1.3 confidently"
  }
};
This $200 experiment could save you from building the wrong product.
7.2 THE PATH FORWARD
IF you validate that structure saves time (per 7.1):

Immediately: Implement Solutions A (Smart Arsenal) and C (Lesson Archetypes)
Week 1: Complete Phase 0 (asset restructuring)
Weeks 2-5: Build V1.3 with 5-10 T1 modules
Week 6: User validation with timed tests

Issue ID: REV_SEQ_01
Severity: BLOCKING
The Problem:
Your pre-requisite order is backwards. You have:
PREQ_01: User Validation (5-stage template)
PREQ_02: Asset Registry (Tier Classification)
PREQ_03: Asset Registry (Stage Mapping)
This is wrong because:

You cannot validate the 5-stage template with users (PREQ_01) until you know which modules you'll show them (PREQ_02 & 03)
If users reject the template, you'll have wasted effort classifying 60 modules you won't use
User validation requires a testable prototype, not just a concept

Corrected Sequence:
javascriptconst CORRECTED_PREREQUISITES = [

javascriptconst PREQ_01_EXPANDED = {

      risk: "Users may feel module selection is too limited"
    },

      action: "IDEAL - Proceed as planned",
      rationale: "Enough variety without overwhelming users"
    },
    
    ifT1Count_16_plus: {
      action: "RE-AUDIT for hidden T2/T3 modules",

      risk: "Non-functional modules will break user trust"
    }
  }
};

⚠️ HIDDEN DEPENDENCY #2: Module Configuration Complexity
Issue ID: REV_DEP_02
Severity: MEDIUM-HIGH
The Problem:
TASK_02 says "implement Smart Arsenal Selector" but doesn't account for module configuration complexity.
The Gap:
Different modules require different configuration. For example:
javascript// Simple module (low setup burden)
{
  id: 12,
  title: "Quick Icebreaker",
  configSchema: {
    question: "string" // Just one text field
  },
  setupTime: "30 seconds"
}

// Complex module (high setup burden)  
{
  id: 1,
  title: "Vocabulary Forge",
  configSchema: {
    vocabularyList: "array<object>", // Need to input 10-20 word/definition pairs
    timeLimit: "number",
    difficulty: "enum"
  },
  setupTime: "5-8 minutes"
}
The Risk:
If most of your T1 modules are "complex," users will still spend 20+ minutes configuring modules, violating the time-savings promise.
Required Addition to PREQ_02:
javascriptconst PREQ_02_EXPANDED = {
  task: "Asset Registry: Stage Compatibility + Complexity Rating",
  
  addToEachModule: {
    compatibleStages: "array<string>", // Already planned
    
    configComplexity: "simple | moderate | complex", // NEW
    
    configComplexityDefinition: {
      simple: "1-3 fields, < 2 min to configure",
      moderate: "4-7 fields, 2-5 min to configure", 
      complex: "> 7 fields OR list inputs, 5-10 min to configure"
    },
    
    setupTimeEstimate: "number (seconds)" // NEW - critical for time budgets
  },
  
  balancingRule: {
    perStage: "Ensure at least 2 'simple' modules in compatibleStages set",
    rationale: "Users need quick-win options to maintain momentum"
  }
};
Why This Matters:
If every T1 module is "complex," your Smart Arsenal won't save time—it'll just shift complexity from module browsing to module configuration.

SECTION 5: RED FLAGS & GOTCHAS
🚩 Red Flag #1: "Static HTML" May Still Be Too Complex
The Risk:
Even "static" HTML export requires:

Module-specific rendering templates (e.g., how does "Vocabulary Forge" render as static HTML?)
Consistent styling across all module types
Image/asset bundling
Cross-browser compatibility

The Gotcha:
You might think "static = simple" but you're really building a template rendering engine. This could be 20-40 hours of work.
Mitigation:
javascriptconst EXPORT_SIMPLIFICATION = {
  mvpApproach: "Render ALL modules as simple formatted text lists",
  
  example: {
    vocabularyForge: `
      <div class="module">
        <h3>Vocabulary Activity</h3>
        <ul>
          ${words.map(w => `<li><strong>${w.word}</strong>: ${w.definition}</li>`)}
        </ul>
      </div>
    `,
    // No fancy tables, no conditional rendering, just text
  },
  
  benefit: "Reduces export complexity by 60%, ships faster"
};

🚩 Red Flag #2: "Autosave" Could Be a Rabbit Hole
The Risk:
TASK_03 mentions autosave, but this can get complex:

Save to where? localStorage? IndexedDB? Server?
How often? Every keystroke? Every 30 seconds?
What about conflicts if user has multiple tabs open?
How do you recover from corrupted autosave data?

The Gotcha:
Autosave is a feature users expect, but it can consume 1-2 weeks of debugging edge cases.
Mitigation:
javascriptconst AUTOSAVE_MVP = {
  approach: "Simple localStorage with no conflict resolution",
  
  implementation: {
    trigger: "Save on blur (when user leaves a field) + every 60 seconds",
    storage: "localStorage.setItem('currentLesson', JSON.stringify(lessonData))",
    recovery: "On page load, check localStorage and offer to 'Resume' or 'Start New'",
    edgeCases: "Accept data loss in edge cases - don't over-engineer"
  },
  
  timeInvestment: "2-3 days max, not 2 weeks"
};

🚩 Red Flag #3: Deferred Scope May Creep Back
The Risk:
You've explicitly deferred:

Full 60-module integration
Interactive export
Lesson Archetypes
AI features

The Gotcha:
During development, you'll be tempted to add "just one more module" or "simple interactivity in export." This is how projects derail.
Mitigation:
javascriptconst SCOPE_PROTECTION = {
  rule: "Any addition not in Sprint 1 plan requires Mr. Hobbs approval + timeline extension",
  
  bannedPhrases: [
    "While we're at it, let's also...",
    "This would only take a few hours...",
    "It's basically already done, we just need to..."
  ],
  
  mantra: "Ship V1.3, validate, THEN add features"
};

/**
 * ===================================================================
 * NET LESSON ASSEMBLER V1.3.1 - CRITICAL FIXES APPLIED
 * ===================================================================
 * FIXES APPLIED:
 * - FIX-001: Bootstrap timing race condition
 * - FIX-002: Critical error message visibility
 * - FIX-003: SRI hash validation
 * - FIX-004: Sanitization bypass protection

(function(window, document) {
    'use strict';

    // --- Configuration (FIXED: Real SRI hashes, configurable fallbacks) ---
    const CONFIG = {
        APP_ROOT_ID: 'lesson-assembler-root',
        AUTOSAVE_KEY: 'net_lesson_assembler_draft',
        AUTOSAVE_INTERVAL: 5000,
        MAX_LOCALSTORAGE_BYTES: 4.5 * 1024 * 1024,
        
        // FIX-003: Use real SRI hashes or set to null to skip validation
        DOMPURIFY_CDN: 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/dompurify/3.0.6/purify.min.js',
        DOMPURIFY_SRI: null, // Set to actual hash or null
        
        JSZIP_CDN: 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jszip/3.10.1/jszip.min.js',
        JSZIP_SRI: null,
        
        AJV_CDN: 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/ajv/8.12.0/ajv7.min.js',
        AJV_SRI: null,
        
        // Configurable fallback paths (deploy-time configuration)
        FALLBACKS: {
            dompurify: [], // Add real paths if available
            jszip: [],
            ajv: []
        },
        
        CHART_JS_URL: 'https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/chart.js@4.4.0/dist/chart.umd.min.js',
        CHART_JS_SRI: null,
        DEFAULT_BRANDING: 'BLUE_SILVER'
    };

    // --- FIX-002: Critical Error Display (Bypass GuardedAPI) ---
    const CriticalErrorDisplay = {
        shown: false,
        
        show(message, details = '') {
            if (this.shown) return; // Only show once
            this.shown = true;
            
            // Create overlay immediately - NO QUEUEING
            const overlay = document.createElement('div');
            overlay.id = 'critical-error-overlay';
            overlay.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 0;
                left: 0;
                right: 0;
                bottom: 0;
                background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.95);
                z-index: 999999;
                display: flex;
                align-items: center;
                justify-content: center;
                font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', sans-serif;
            `;
            
            const content = document.createElement('div');
            content.style.cssText = `
                background: #1a1a1a;
                border: 3px solid #ef476f;
                border-radius: 8px;
                padding: 30px;
                max-width: 600px;
                color: white;
                text-align: center;
            `;
            
            content.innerHTML = `
                <div style="font-size: 48px; margin-bottom: 20px;">⚠️</div>
                <h1 style="color: #ef476f; margin: 0 0 15px 0; font-size: 24px;">
                    EDITOR LOCKED
                </h1>
                <p style="font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.6; margin: 0 0 20px 0;">
                    ${this.escapeHtml(message)}
                </p>
                ${details ? `<pre style="background: #000; padding: 15px; border-radius: 4px; font-size: 12px; text-align: left; overflow-x: auto;">${this.escapeHtml(details)}</pre>` : ''}
                <p style="font-size: 14px; color: #aaa; margin-top: 20px;">
                    The application cannot start safely. Please contact support.
                </p>
            `;
            
            overlay.appendChild(content);
            
            // Inject immediately - before DOMContentLoaded if necessary
            if (document.body) {
                document.body.appendChild(overlay);
            } else {
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
                    document.body.appendChild(overlay);
                });
            }
            
            console.error('[CRITICAL ERROR]', message, details);
        },
        
        escapeHtml(str) {
            const div = document.createElement('div');
            div.textContent = str;
            return div.innerHTML;
        }
    };

    // --- Guarded API V1.1 (Unchanged - Proven Stable) ---
    const GuardedAPI = (() => {
        let isReady = false;
        let initCalled = false;
        const callQueue = [];
        const subscribers = new Map();
        const MAX_QUEUE_SIZE = 100;
        
        const logCore = (msg) => console.log(`[GuardedAPI V1.1] ${msg}`);
        
        const safeCall = (func, context = 'default') => {
            try {
                func();
            } catch (e) {
                console.error(`[GuardedAPI V1.1] Error (${context}):`, e);
                publish('error', { source: 'safeCall', context, error: e });
            }
        };
        
        const publish = (eventName, data) => {
            logCore(`Publishing: ${eventName}`);
            if (subscribers.has(eventName)) {
                subscribers.get(eventName).forEach(cb => {
                    safeCall(() => cb(data), `publish:${eventName}`);
                });
            }
        };
        
        const init = () => {
            if (initCalled || isReady) return;
            initCalled = true;
            logCore("Initializing...");
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                isReady = true;
                logCore(`Ready. Processing ${callQueue.length} queued operations...`);
                
                while (callQueue.length > 0) {
                    safeCall(callQueue.shift(), 'queue');
                }
                
                publish('ready');
            }, 50);
        };
        
        const on = (eventName, callback) => {
            if (typeof callback !== 'function') return () => {};
            
            if (!subscribers.has(eventName)) {
                subscribers.set(eventName, new Map());
            }
            
            const subId = Symbol('subId');
            subscribers.get(eventName).set(subId, callback);
            logCore(`Subscribed: ${eventName}`);
            
            return () => {
                if (subscribers.has(eventName) && subscribers.get(eventName).delete(subId)) {
                    logCore(`Unsubscribed: ${eventName}`);
                }
            };
        };
        
        const execute = (func) => {
            if (typeof func !== 'function') return;
            
            if (isReady) {
                safeCall(func, 'executeImmediate');
            } else {
                if (callQueue.length >= MAX_QUEUE_SIZE) {
                    console.warn(`[GuardedAPI V1.1] Queue full (${MAX_QUEUE_SIZE}). Discarding.`);
                    publish('error', { source: 'execute', error: 'Queue full' });
                    return;
                }
                callQueue.push(func);
            }
        };
        
        const publicAPI = { init, on, execute, publish };
        window.__NET_API_V1_3_1 = publicAPI;
        return publicAPI;
    })();

    // --- FIX-001: Initialize GuardedAPI IMMEDIATELY ---
    GuardedAPI.init();

    // --- Robust Dependency Loader (Unchanged - Already Solid) ---
    function loadDependency({
        name = 'dep',
        cdnUrl = '',
        sri = '',
        fallbacks = [],
        maxRetries = 2,
        initialDelayMs = 300,
        attributes = {}
    } = {}) {
        if (!cdnUrl && (!fallbacks || fallbacks.length === 0)) {
            return Promise.reject(new Error(`No URLs provided for ${name}`));
        }
        
        const findExistingScript = (src) => {
            try {
                const scripts = Array.from(document.scripts || []);
                for (const s of scripts) {
                    if (s.src && new URL(s.src, location.href).toString() === new URL(src, location.href).toString()) {
                        return s;
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                console.warn('[Loader] URL comparison failed:', e);
            }
            return null;
        };
        
        const inject = (url, sriAttr) => new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const existing = findExistingScript(url);
            
            if (existing) {
                if (existing.dataset._loaded === 'true') {
                    return resolve(existing);
                }
                
                existing.addEventListener('load', () => {
                    existing.dataset._loaded = 'true';
                    resolve(existing);
                }, { once: true });
                
                existing.addEventListener('error', () => {
                    reject(new Error(`Existing script failed: ${url}`));
                }, { once: true });
                
                return;
            }
            
            const el = document.createElement('script');
            el.src = url;
            el.async = true;
            
            // FIX-003: Only apply SRI if hash is provided
            if (sriAttr && sriAttr.trim()) {
                el.integrity = sriAttr;
                el.crossOrigin = 'anonymous';
            }
            
            Object.entries(attributes).forEach(([k, v]) => el.setAttribute(k, v));
            
            el.addEventListener('load', () => {
                el.dataset._loaded = 'true';
                resolve(el);
            }, { once: true });
            
            el.addEventListener('error', () => {
                try {
                    el.remove();
                } catch (e) {}
                reject(new Error(`Failed to load ${url}`));
            }, { once: true });
            
            document.head.appendChild(el);
        });
        
        const retryCdn = async (url, sriAttr, attempts, delay) => {
            let lastErr;
            
            for (let i = 0; i < attempts; i++) {
                if (i > 0) {
                    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, delay * Math.pow(2, i - 1)));
                }
                
                try {
                    return await inject(url, sriAttr);
                } catch (err) {
                    console.warn(`[Loader] CDN attempt ${i + 1}/${attempts} failed for ${name}: ${err.message}`);
                    lastErr = err;
                }
            }
            
            throw lastErr;
        };
        
        const tryFallbacks = async (list) => {
            let lastErr;
            
            for (const fb of list) {
                try {
                    return await inject(fb, null);
                } catch (err) {
                    console.warn(`[Loader] Fallback ${fb} failed for ${name}: ${err.message}`);
                    lastErr = err;
                }
            }
            
            throw lastErr || new Error('No fallbacks succeeded');
        };
        
        return new Promise(async (resolve, reject) => {
            try {
                // Try CDN first
                if (cdnUrl) {
                    try {
                        return resolve(await retryCdn(cdnUrl, sri, maxRetries, initialDelayMs));
                    } catch (cdnErr) {
                        console.warn(`[Loader] All CDN attempts failed for ${name}: ${cdnErr.message}`);
                    }
                }
                
                // Try fallbacks
                if (fallbacks && fallbacks.length) {
                    try {
                        return resolve(await tryFallbacks(fallbacks));
                    } catch (fbErr) {
                        return reject(new Error(`All attempts failed for ${name}: ${fbErr.message}`));
                    }
                } else {
                    return reject(new Error(`CDN failed and no fallbacks configured for ${name}`));
                }
            } catch (outer) {
                reject(new Error(`Loader error for ${name}: ${outer.message}`));
            }
        });
    }

    // --- IndexedDB Wrapper (Unchanged - Already Solid) ---
    const IDBWrapper = (() => {
        const DB_NAME = 'net_lesson_assembler_db';
        const STORE = 'drafts';
        const VERSION = 1;
        
        const openDB = () => new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            try {
                const req = indexedDB.open(DB_NAME, VERSION);
                
                req.onupgradeneeded = e => {
                    if (!e.target.result.objectStoreNames.contains(STORE)) {
                        e.target.result.createObjectStore(STORE, { keyPath: 'id' });
                    }
                };
                
                req.onsuccess = e => resolve(e.target.result);
                req.onerror = e => reject(e.target.error || 'IDB open fail');
            } catch (err) {
                reject(err);
            }
        });
        
        const op = (mode, action) => openDB().then(db => new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const tx = db.transaction(STORE, mode);
            action(tx.objectStore(STORE));
            tx.oncomplete = () => resolve(true);
            tx.onerror = e => reject(e.target.error || `IDB ${mode} fail`);
        }));
        
        const put = (id, data) => op('readwrite', st => st.put({
            id,
            data,
            updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
        }));
        
        const get = (id) => openDB().then(db => new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const r = db.transaction(STORE, 'readonly').objectStore(STORE).get(id);
            r.onsuccess = e => resolve(e.target.result ? e.target.result.data : null);
            r.onerror = e => reject(e.target.error || 'IDB get fail');
        }));
        
        const remove = (id) => op('readwrite', st => st.delete(id));
        
        const keys = () => openDB().then(db => new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const r = db.transaction(STORE, 'readonly').objectStore(STORE).getAllKeys();
            r.onsuccess = e => resolve(e.target.result || []);
            r.onerror = e => reject(e.target.error || 'IDB keys fail');
        }));
        
        return { put, get, remove, keys, openDB };
    })();

    // --- FIX-002: Sanitization & Editor Locking (FIXED) ---
    let SANITIZER_STATE = {
        available: false,
        initialized: false,
        locked: false
    };

    function disableEditorUI(reason = 'Sanitizer unavailable') {
        if (SANITIZER_STATE.locked) return;
        SANITIZER_STATE.locked = true;
        
        // FIX-002: Show critical error IMMEDIATELY (bypass GuardedAPI)
        CriticalErrorDisplay.show(
            `Security library failed to load: ${reason}`,
            'The editor has been locked to prevent unsafe content creation.'
        );
        
        // Queue the actual element disabling (non-critical)
        GuardedAPI.execute(() => {
            logApp(`Disabling editor UI: ${reason}`);
            
            document.querySelectorAll(
                'input:not([data-keep-editable]), ' +
                'textarea:not([data-keep-editable]), ' +
                'select:not([data-keep-editable]), ' +
                '[contenteditable="true"]:not([data-keep-editable]), ' +
                'button:not([data-keep-editable])'
            ).forEach(el => {
                try {
                    el.disabled = true;
                    el.setAttribute('aria-disabled', 'true');
                } catch (e) {
                    console.warn('Failed to disable element:', e);
                }
            });
        });
    }

    function enableEditorUI() {
        if (!SANITIZER_STATE.available || !SANITIZER_STATE.initialized) {
            logApp("Cannot enable editor - Sanitizer not confirmed.");
            return;
        }
        
        SANITIZER_STATE.locked = false;
        
        GuardedAPI.execute(() => {
            logApp("Enabling editor UI.");
            
            document.querySelectorAll(
                'input:not([data-keep-editable]), ' +
                'textarea:not([data-keep-editable]), ' +
                'select:not([data-keep-editable]), ' +
                '[contenteditable="true"]:not([data-keep-editable]), ' +
                'button:not([data-keep-editable])'
            ).forEach(el => {
                try {
                    el.disabled = false;
                    el.removeAttribute('aria-disabled');
                } catch (e) {
                    console.warn('Failed to enable element:', e);
                }
            });
            
            showNotification('Editing enabled - Sanitizer ready', 'success');
        });
    }

    // FIX-004: Hardened sanitization policy
    function sanitizeHTMLStrict(html) {
        if (!SANITIZER_STATE.initialized) {
            console.warn("Sanitization attempted before initialization.");
            disableEditorUI('Sanitizer not initialized');
            throw new Error('Sanitizer initialization incomplete.');
        }
        
        if (SANITIZER_STATE.available && typeof DOMPurify !== 'undefined') {
            const policy = {
                USE_PROFILES: { html: true },
                
                // Strict attribute blocking
                FORBID_ATTR: [
                    'onerror', 'onload', 'onclick', 'onmouseover', 'onfocus',
                    'onblur', 'oninput', 'onchange', 'onsubmit', 'onreset',
                    'style', 'formaction', 'action', 'method'
                ],
                
                // Strict tag blocking
                FORBID_TAGS: [
                    'style', 'link', 'iframe', 'script', 'object', 'embed',
                    'form', 'input', 'button', 'select', 'textarea', 'meta',
                    'base', 'frame', 'frameset'
                ],
                
                // Strict URI validation
                ALLOWED_URI_REGEXP: /^(?:(?:https?|mailto|tel):|[^a-z]|[a-z+.-]+(?:[^a-z+.-:]|$))/i,
                
                // No data attributes
                ALLOW_DATA_ATTRIBUTES: false,
                
                // Additional security
                SAFE_FOR_TEMPLATES: true,
                WHOLE_DOCUMENT: false,
                RETURN_DOM: false,
                RETURN_DOM_FRAGMENT: false
            };
            
            return DOMPurify.sanitize(html, policy);
        } else {
            disableEditorUI('Sanitizer unavailable');
            throw new Error('Sanitizer unavailable.');
        }
    }

    // --- Validation (Unchanged - Already Solid) ---
    let validator = { validate: null, engine: null, ready: false };

    function getLessonSchema() {
        return {
            type: 'object',
            properties: {
                schemaVersion: { type: 'string' },
                title: { type: 'string', minLength: 1 },
                createdAt: { type: 'string', format: 'date-time' },
                updatedAt: { type: 'string', format: 'date-time' },
                stages: {
                    type: 'array',
                    minItems: 1,
                    items: {
                        type: 'object',
                        properties: {
                            id: { type: 'string' },
                            title: { type: 'string' },
                            content: { type: 'string' },
                            arsenalIds: {
                                type: 'array',
                                items: { type: 'number' }
                            }
                        },
                        required: ['id', 'content'],
                        additionalProperties: true
                    }
                }
            },
            required: ['schemaVersion', 'title', 'stages', 'createdAt', 'updatedAt'],
            additionalProperties: false
        };
    }

    function fallbackValidateLesson(data) {
        if (!data || typeof data !== 'object') {
            return { valid: false, errors: [{ message: 'Data is not an object' }] };
        }
        
        const requiredRoot = ['schemaVersion', 'title', 'stages', 'createdAt', 'updatedAt'];
        for (const k of requiredRoot) {
            if (!(k in data)) {
                return { valid: false, errors: [{ message: `Missing root field: ${k}` }] };
            }
        }
        
        if (!Array.isArray(data.stages) || data.stages.length < 1) {
            return { valid: false, errors: [{ message: 'stages must be non-empty array' }] };
        }
        
        for (const [i, stage] of data.stages.entries()) {
            if (!stage || typeof stage !== 'object') {
                return { valid: false, errors: [{ message: `Stage ${i} is not an object` }] };
            }
            
            const requiredStage = ['id', 'content'];
            for (const k of requiredStage) {
                if (!(k in stage)) {
                    return { valid: false, errors: [{ message: `Stage ${i} missing field: ${k}` }] };
                }
            }
            
            if ('arsenalIds' in stage && !Array.isArray(stage.arsenalIds)) {
                return { valid: false, errors: [{ message: `Stage ${i} arsenalIds must be array` }] };
            }
        }
        
        return { valid: true, errors: [] };
    }

    async function ensureValidator() {
        if (validator.ready) return;
        
        logApp("Ensuring validator...");
        
        try {
            // Check if AJV already loaded
            if (typeof Ajv !== 'undefined') {
                const ajv = new Ajv({ allErrors: true });
                const schema = getLessonSchema();
                const validateFn = ajv.compile(schema);
                
                validator = {
                    validate: data => ({
                        valid: validateFn(data),
                        errors: validateFn.errors || []
                    }),
                    engine: 'ajv',
                    ready: true
                };
                
                logApp("AJV validator ready (pre-loaded).");
                return;
            }
            
            // Attempt to load AJV
            await loadDependency({
                name: 'ajv',
                cdnUrl: CONFIG.AJV_CDN,
                sri: CONFIG.AJV_SRI,
                fallbacks: CONFIG.FALLBACKS.ajv
            });
            
            if (typeof Ajv !== 'undefined') {
                const ajv = new Ajv({ allErrors: true });
                const schema = getLessonSchema();
                const validateFn = ajv.compile(schema);
                
                validator = {
                    validate: data => ({
                        valid: validateFn(data),
                        errors: validateFn.errors || []
                    }),
                    engine: 'ajv',
                    ready: true
                };
                
                logApp("AJV validator ready (loaded dynamically).");
                return;
            } else {
                throw new Error("AJV loaded but global not found");
            }
        } catch (e) {
            logApp(`AJV load failed (${e.message}), using fallback validator.`, "warn");
        }
        
        // Use fallback validator
        validator = {
            validate: fallbackValidateLesson,
            engine: 'fallback',
            ready: true
        };
        
        logApp("Fallback validator ready.");
    }

    // --- Utility: Notification ---
    function showNotification(msg, type = 'info') {
        try {
            GuardedAPI.execute(() => {
                let area = document.getElementById('notification-area');
                
                if (!area) {
                    area = document.createElement('div');
                    area.id = 'notification-area';
                    area.style.cssText = `
                        position: fixed;
                        bottom: 10px;
                        left: 10px;
                        z-index: 10000;
                        display: flex;
                        flex-direction: column;
                        gap: 5px;
                    `;
                    document.body.appendChild(area);
                }
                
                const note = document.createElement('div');
                note.textContent = msg;
                note.style.cssText = `
                    padding: 10px 15px;
                    border-radius: 5px;
                    box-shadow: 0 2px 5px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
                    color: white;
                    font-size: 14px;
                `;
                
                note.style.backgroundColor = 
                    type === 'error' ? '#ef476f' :
                    type === 'success' ? '#06d6a0' : '#3B82F6';
                
                area.appendChild(note);
                
                setTimeout(() => {
                    try {
                        note.remove();
                    } catch (e) {}
                }, 4000);
            });
        } catch (e) {
            console.log('[notify]', msg);
        }
    }

    // --- Core Application Logic ---
    let currentLessonData = null;
    let autosaveIntervalId = null;
    const dependenciesLoaded = { dompurify: false, jszip: false, ajv: false };

    const logApp = (msg, type = "info") => {
        const prefix = '[Assembler V1.3.1]';
        if (type === 'error') console.error(prefix, msg);
        else if (type === 'warn') console.warn(prefix, msg);
        else console.log(prefix, msg);
    };

    // --- Persistence (Validated) ---
    async function saveDraftPatched(dataToSave) {
        if (!dataToSave) return false;
        
        if (!validator.ready) await ensureValidator();
        
        const validationResult = validator.validate(dataToSave);
        
        if (!validationResult.valid) {
            logApp(`Draft validation failed (${validator.engine}). Cannot save.`, "error");
            console.error("Validation Errors:", validationResult.errors);
            showNotification('Draft invalid. Cannot save.', 'error');
            return false;
        }
        
        const dataString = JSON.stringify(dataToSave);
        
        try {
            if (dataString.length <= CONFIG.MAX_LOCALSTORAGE_BYTES) {
                localStorage.setItem(CONFIG.AUTOSAVE_KEY, dataString);
                logApp("Draft saved (localStorage).");
                
                // Clean up IDB if we're back under the limit
                GuardedAPI.execute(() => {
                    IDBWrapper.remove(CONFIG.AUTOSAVE_KEY).catch(e => {});
                });
                
                return true;
            } else {
                logApp("Draft size exceeds localStorage limit. Using IndexedDB.");
                
                await IDBWrapper.put(CONFIG.AUTOSAVE_KEY, dataToSave);
                
                // Clean up localStorage
                GuardedAPI.execute(() => {
                    try {
                        localStorage.removeItem(CONFIG.AUTOSAVE_KEY);
                    } catch (e) {}
                });
                
                logApp("Draft saved (IndexedDB).");
                return true;
            }
        } catch (e) {
            logApp("Error saving draft.", "error");
            console.error(e);
            showNotification('Error saving draft.', 'error');
            return false;
        }
    }

    async function loadDraftPatched() {
        if (!validator.ready) await ensureValidator();
        
        let loadedData = null;
        let source = null;
        
        // Try IndexedDB first (handles large lessons)
        try {
            const idbData = await IDBWrapper.get(CONFIG.AUTOSAVE_KEY);
            
            if (idbData) {
                const res = validator.validate(idbData);
                
                if (res.valid) {
                    loadedData = idbData;
                    source = 'IndexedDB';
                    logApp(`Validated draft loaded from ${source}.`);
                } else {
                    console.warn(`IDB draft invalid (${validator.engine}). Discarding.`, res.errors);
                    GuardedAPI.execute(() => {
                        IDBWrapper.remove(CONFIG.AUTOSAVE_KEY).catch(e => {});
                    });
                }
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.warn('IDB load failed:', e);
        }
        
        // Try localStorage if IDB failed
        if (!loadedData) {
            try {
                const s = localStorage.getItem(CONFIG.AUTOSAVE_KEY);
                
                if (s) {
                    try {
                        const parsed = JSON.parse(s);
                        const res = validator.validate(parsed);
                        
                        if (res.valid) {
                            loadedData = parsed;
                            source = 'localStorage';
                            logApp(`Validated draft loaded from ${source}.`);
                        } else {
                            console.warn(`LS draft invalid (${validator.engine}). Discarding.`, res.errors);
                            GuardedAPI.execute(() => {
                                localStorage.removeItem(CONFIG.AUTOSAVE_KEY);
                            });
                        }
                    } catch (e) {
                        console.warn('Parsing LS draft failed. Discarding.', e);
                        GuardedAPI.execute(() => {
                            localStorage.removeItem(CONFIG.AUTOSAVE_KEY);
                        });
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                console.warn('LS read failed:', e);
            }
        }
        
        if (loadedData) {
            showNotification(`Draft loaded from ${source}`, 'info');
            return loadedData;
        }
        
        logApp("No valid draft found.");
        return null;
    }

Initial Observations
This document represents a simulated multi-agent audit process for a educational software tool called the "NET Lesson Assembler V1.3". Let me break down what's happening here and provide my analytical thoughts:

2. Technical Artifact: A JavaScript-based Lesson Planning Tool
The actual code is a client-side web application for educators to:

Create structured lesson plans following a specific curriculum template
Integrate pre-built "Arsenal" teaching modules
Export lessons as downloadable ZIP packages
Persist drafts using localStorage or IndexedDB
Architecture Analysis
Core Components:
GuardedAPI Pattern (V1.1)
Event-driven initialization system
Queue management for pre-initialization calls
Pub/sub messaging
Intent: Prevent race conditions during app startup
Dependency Management (PR-A)
CDN loading with retry logic
SRI (Subresource Integrity) validation
Local fallback paths
Critical Libraries: DOMPurify, JSZip, AJV (JSON Schema validator)
Security Layer (PR-B)
HTML sanitization via DOMPurify
UI lockdown mechanism if sanitizer fails
Philosophy: "Fail closed" - disable editing if security cannot be guaranteed

Schema validation before save

Validation System (PR-D)

Critical Thinking: What Are The REAL Issues?
🔴 HIGH SEVERITY ISSUES
1. Bootstrap Timing Race Condition
javascript
async function bootstrap() {
    await ensureCriticalDependencies(); // Async
    const loadedDraft = await loadDraftPatched();
    
    if (!SANITIZER_STATE.locked) {
        GuardedAPI.execute(renderAssemblerUI); // Queued!
        GuardedAPI.execute(() => startAutosavePatched(...));
    }
    
    // PROBLEM: GuardedAPI.init() is called AFTER bootstrap completes
    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', GuardedAPI.init);
    } else {
        GuardedAPI.init(); // Called synchronously, but AFTER execute() calls
    }
}
The Flaw:

GuardedAPI.execute() queues operations
GuardedAPI.init() processes the queue
But init() is called at the END of bootstrap()
If DOMPurify fails during ensureCriticalDependencies(), disableEditorUI() tries to use GuardedAPI.execute() before the API is initialized
Result: Critical error messages may never display
Databank1's Likely Concern: This is exactly what they would flag.

2. Editor Lock Message Visibility
javascript
function disableEditorUI(reason = 'Sanitizer unavailable') {
    if (SANITIZER_STATE.locked) return;
    SANITIZER_STATE.locked = true;
    try {
        GuardedAPI.execute(() => { // ⚠️ QUEUED - may never run
            logApp(`Disabling editor: ${reason}`);
            // ... disable elements
            showNotification(`Editing disabled: ${reason}`, 'error');
        });
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('disableEditorUI error', e);
    }
}
The Problem:

If called before GuardedAPI.init(), this gets queued indefinitely
User sees a blank screen with no explanation
Security Impact: User might assume the app is working when it's actually locked
Fix: Critical safety messages should bypass the queue:

javascript
function disableEditorUI(reason) {
    SANITIZER_STATE.locked = true;
    
    // IMMEDIATE notification (don't queue critical errors)
    const msg = document.createElement('div');
    msg.textContent = `EDITOR LOCKED: ${reason}`;
    msg.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:0;left:0;right:0;background:crimson;color:white;padding:20px;z-index:99999;text-align:center;font-size:18px;';
    document.body.appendChild(msg);
    
    // Then queue the actual element disabling
    GuardedAPI.execute(() => {
        document.querySelectorAll('input, textarea, select, button').forEach(el => {
            el.disabled = true;
        });
    });
}
🟡 MEDIUM SEVERITY ISSUES
3. SRI Integrity Hash Placeholders
javascript
DOMPURIFY_SRI: 'sha256-QucImAfk/+nlCNvoGg7W0lUAmh1CFYl3h7L/JFFM7yM=', // Example
JSZIP_SRI: 'sha256-bSQz99/d05b02nQx4x7G5J/oFrZlJ+nO+c/04o2wH48=', // Example
Comments say "Example" - these need to be real hashes or removed entirely. Fake SRI hashes will cause all CDN loads to fail.

4. Fallback Paths Are Fictional
javascript
FALLBACKS: {
    dompurify: ['/vendor/dompurify.min.js', '/static/vendor/dompurify.min.js'],
    jszip: ['/vendor/jszip.min.js', '/static/vendor/jszip.min.js'],
    ajv: ['/vendor/ajv.min.js']
}
These paths don't exist unless explicitly set up. The app will always fail if CDN is unreachable.

5. Asset Registry is Empty
javascript
ARSENAL_CONCEPTS: [ /* ... (Include full 60 concepts array) ... */
    { id: 1, title: "The Vocabulary Forge", focus: "Confidence Engine", icon: "🔥", category: "arsenal", description: "Timed game: spell/use vocab." },
    // ...
    { id: 60, title: "The 6-Word Story", ... }
]
Only 2 of 60 arsenal modules are defined. The actual lesson rendering will mostly show "Module X not found" errors.

Dependency Loader is Solid: The retry logic, SRI validation, and fallback chain are well-designed
IndexedDB Fallback is Smart: Automatically handles large lesson files
Validation Strategy is Sound: AJV with manual fallback ensures data integrity
Security-First Mindset: The "disable editor on sanitizer failure" approach is correct (execution just needs fixing)

The irony is that the extensive safety mechanisms (sanitization locks, validation, guarded API) actually create new failure modes due to their interdependencies.

/**
 * ===================================================================
 * AIPetModule V2.0 - SECURITY HARDENED
 * ===================================================================
 * SECURITY FIXES APPLIED:
 * - SEC-001: XSS Prevention via DOMPurify sanitization
 * - SEC-002: All DOM operations queued through GuardedAPI
 * - SEC-003: Async error handling with try-catch
 * - SEC-004: Production logging controls
 * - SEC-005: Event authentication and validation
 * - SEC-006: CSP compliance (no inline handlers)
 * - SEC-007: Event debouncing for DoS protection
 * - SEC-008: Secure lifecycle management with cleanup
 * - SEC-009: Input validation with schema enforcement
 * - SEC-010: Rate limiting on event processing
 * ===================================================================
 */

(function(window) {
    'use strict';

    // --- Configuration ---
    const CONFIG = {
        MODULE_NAME: 'AIPetModule',
        VERSION: '2.0.0',
        DOMPURIFY_CDN: 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/dompurify/3.0.6/purify.min.js',
        DEBOUNCE_DELAY_MS: 300,
        MAX_EVENTS_PER_SECOND: 10,
        EVENT_AUTH_TOKEN: null, // Set via init() options
        PRODUCTION_MODE: true,  // Disable verbose logs in production
        PANEL_ID: 'ai-pet-status-panel',
        STYLE_ID: 'ai-pet-module-styles'
    };

    // --- SEC-004: Controlled Logging ---
    const Logger = {
        log(msg, data = null) {
            if (!CONFIG.PRODUCTION_MODE) {
                console.log(`[${CONFIG.MODULE_NAME} V${CONFIG.VERSION}]`, msg, data || '');
            }
        },
        
        warn(msg, data = null) {
            console.warn(`[${CONFIG.MODULE_NAME}]`, msg, data || '');
        },
        
        error(msg, error = null) {
            // Always log errors (sanitized)
            console.error(`[${CONFIG.MODULE_NAME}] ERROR:`, msg);
            if (error && !CONFIG.PRODUCTION_MODE) {
                console.error('Details:', error);
            }
        }
    };

    // --- SEC-001: Sanitization Layer ---
    let sanitizerReady = false;
    let sanitizerLoading = false;

    async function ensureSanitizer() {
        if (sanitizerReady) return true;
        if (sanitizerLoading) {
            // Wait for existing load attempt
            await new Promise(resolve => {
                const check = setInterval(() => {
                    if (sanitizerReady || !sanitizerLoading) {
                        clearInterval(check);
                        resolve();
                    }
                }, 50);
            });
            return sanitizerReady;
        }

        if (typeof DOMPurify !== 'undefined') {
            sanitizerReady = true;
            Logger.log('DOMPurify already available');
            return true;
        }

        sanitizerLoading = true;
        Logger.log('Loading DOMPurify...');

        return new Promise((resolve) => {
            const script = document.createElement('script');
            script.src = CONFIG.DOMPURIFY_CDN;
            script.async = true;
            script.crossOrigin = 'anonymous';

            script.onload = () => {
                sanitizerReady = typeof DOMPurify !== 'undefined';
                sanitizerLoading = false;
                
                if (sanitizerReady) {
                    Logger.log('DOMPurify loaded successfully');
                    resolve(true);
                } else {
                    Logger.error('DOMPurify failed to initialize');
                    resolve(false);
                }
            };

            script.onerror = () => {
                Logger.error('Failed to load DOMPurify from CDN');
                sanitizerLoading = false;
                resolve(false);
            };

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        });
    }

    function sanitizeHTML(html) {
        if (!sanitizerReady || typeof DOMPurify === 'undefined') {
            Logger.error('Sanitizer not ready - returning empty string');
            return '';
        }

        // SEC-001: Strict sanitization policy
        return DOMPurify.sanitize(html, {
            ALLOWED_TAGS: ['p', 'br', 'strong', 'em', 'span', 'div'],
            ALLOWED_ATTR: ['class'],
            FORBID_ATTR: [
                'onerror',

/**
 * ===================================================================
 * NET LESSON ASSEMBLER V1.3.1 - CRITICAL FIXES APPLIED
